- **Re-merge ``file_hash`` invariant tests (Step 77 / MRG-08a; Plan §10.5 step 5, §15.1):** New `TestReMergeHashInvariants` class in `tests/backend/test_sample_merge.py` (3 cases) locks the Plan §10.5 step 5 ``SHA-256(S1.file_hash ‖ S2.file_hash ‖ strategy ‖ SAMPLE_SCHEMA_VERSION)`` recipe at the integration level by driving the live `merge_samples` round-trip twice (or three times) per assertion, complementing the unit-level `TestFileHashRecipe` class that already exercises `_compute_file_hash` directly. Cases: (i) **same sources + same order + same strategy → identical `samples.file_hash` + matching provenance** — two back-to-back `merge_samples` calls allocate two distinct `samples` row ids (Plan §10.5: "the new merged sample has a distinct identity in `samples`" — only the deterministic `file_hash` carries across), but the two merged DBs' `merge_provenance` rows hold byte-identical `strategy` (`flag_only`), `source_sample_ids` JSON (`[s1_id, s2_id]`), `source_file_hashes` JSON (`["hash_s1", "hash_s2"]`), and `concordance_summary` JSON; a paired sanity assertion locks that the round-trip hash equals `_compute_file_hash("hash_s1", "hash_s2", FLAG_ONLY)` so a future regression that drifts the integration-level recipe away from the unit-level recipe surfaces immediately. (ii) **Changing strategy changes `file_hash`** — re-merging the same sources under all three Plan §10.3 strategies (`flag_only`, `prefer_23andme`, `prefer_ancestrydna`) produces three distinct hashes (`len(set(hashes.values())) == 3`), so the wizard's "regenerate under a different strategy" flow per Plan §10.5 "Re-merge" paragraph cannot collide with the existing merged sample's identity — protects the user from a silent overwrite when they switch strategies on an already-merged individual. (iii) **Swapping source order changes `file_hash`** — merging `[s1, s2]` then `[s2, s1]` produces distinct hashes because `_compute_file_hash` concatenates left-to-right, which is order-sensitive on purpose (Plan §10.5: "order-sensitive on purpose ... merging [A, B] and [B, A] yield different merged content and therefore must yield different file_hashes"); paired provenance assertions lock that `source_sample_ids` and `source_file_hashes` mirror the request order in both directions (forward: `[s1_id, s2_id]` / `["hash_s1", "hash_s2"]`; reverse: `[s2_id, s1_id]` / `["hash_s2", "hash_s1"]`) — the swap genuinely flips both sides of the SHA-256 input, not just the recorded metadata. The fixture (`merged_setup`) reuses `TestHappyPath`'s canonical seven-locus `S1_VARIANTS` / `S2_VARIANTS` bucket coverage and the existing `_create_source_sample` / `_seed_installed_vep_bundle` / `_noop_annotation_enqueue` helpers — no new fixtures or helpers introduced (the round-trip determinism is a property of the merge pipeline, not of the test data; switching to the dual-upload fixture from Step 75 would add no new signal because the recipe inputs are the source samples' `file_hash` strings, the strategy enum, and the schema version constant — not the merged row content). Per CLAUDE.md SOP #8 the targeted local-test policy applied (Step 77 is not in the cross-cutting full-sweep set, isn't an Alembic migration, and doesn't touch `backend/db/sample_schema.py` or `backend/db/tables.py`); `pytest tests/backend/test_sample_merge.py tests/backend/test_sample_merge_preview.py tests/backend/test_merge_routes.py` ran green (86 cases in ~88 s) and `ruff check tests/backend/test_sample_merge.py` is clean. Risk register: R-12 (genotype concordance / data integrity) is the load-bearing item — `samples.file_hash` is what Settings → Samples + the backup/restore tarball use to spot legacy-vs-merged identity drift, so locking the determinism contract at the integration level (not just the unit level) prevents a regression where the recipe is silently shadowed by a wrapper that re-derives the hash differently when called twice; R-19 (re-annotation / findings drift) is the secondary item — swap-order distinctness ensures that a user who picks `[A, B]` vs `[B, A]` in the merge wizard sees two genuinely separate merged samples in the registry rather than a silent overwrite that would also blow away the annotation cascade attached to the prior merge. No CLAUDE.md SOP #2 Context7 invocation needed: pure pytest + SQLAlchemy Core + standard library patterns already established throughout the existing merge tests. No frontend changes, no backend code changes — Step 77 is a tests-only step extending the existing file. No OpenAPI update (the route surface is unchanged from Step 68). The follow-on Step 78 / MRG-08c lands the annotation-engine cross-PK test that asserts annotation output is byte-identical across merged ((chrom, pos) PK) and unmerged (rsid PK) sample DBs.

- **Merge semantics tests against the dual-upload fixture (Step 76 / MRG-08; Plan §10.2, §10.3, §15.1):** New test surface in `tests/backend/test_sample_merge.py` (19 cases across three new classes) parametrizes the three Plan §10.3 strategies (`flag_only`, `prefer_23andme`, `prefer_ancestrydna`) against the hand-curated 19-locus dual-upload fixture from Step 75 and against synthetic ``_apply_semantics`` calls for the indel-vs-indel and allele-order edge cases that the fixture's no-indel-row design deliberately doesn't carry. `TestDualUploadFixtureMergeSemantics` loads `tests/fixtures/sample_dual_upload_individual/{23andme.txt, ancestrydna.txt, expected_concordance.json}` via the vendor-specific parsers (`parse_23andme` / `parse_ancestrydna` directly, not `dispatcher.parse` — the AncestryDNA leg's `# Pairs with sample_dual_upload_individual/23andme.txt` comment trips the dispatcher's `_23ANDME_SUBSTRING` substring detector and mis-routes the file; this is documented inline in `_load_dual_fixture_variants` and noted as a residual fixture/dispatcher TODO that's out of scope for Step 76), materializes both source sample DBs via the existing `_create_source_sample` helper, runs `merge_samples` for each strategy, and asserts: (a) `concordance_summary` bucket counts match `expected_concordance.json` within ±1% per Plan §15.1 MRG-08 (`_within_one_percent(actual, expected)` uses `max(1, ceil(0.01 * expected))` so the band rounds to 1 for the small 19-locus fixture but scales linearly to a larger fixture without rewriting); (b) row-count invariant `match + filled_nocall + discordant + unique_S1 + unique_S2 == total_merged_loci == 19` (Plan §10.4(c) — `collapsed_rsid` is an additive marker, not part of the sum); (c) per-locus outcomes match the gold standard's per-locus block (`rsid` / `genotype` / `source` / `concordance` / `discordant_alt_genotype` / `alt_rsid`) — for discordant loci pulling the strategy-specific `strategy_outcomes` triple, for non-discordant loci pulling the top-level `source`/`concordance` (top-level `source` is absent at discordant loci by JSON design, since strategy decides; the test's `top_source = locus.get("source")` handles this branch explicitly); (d) `flag_only` writes the paired `S1=<gt>;S2=<gt>` encoding at every discordant locus and ` prefer_*` writes only the loser's call (single-key `S1=<gt>` or `S2=<gt>`, never paired). At rsid-collapse loci where neither rsid is in the test harness's empty VEP bundle, the S1 tiebreaker convention (`_resolve_winner` fallback) is asserted to fire and `alt_rsid` carries the loser. `TestAlleleOrderNormalization` and `TestIndelDiscordance` exercise `_apply_semantics` directly with synthetic two-coord inputs to lock the Plan §10.2 step 3 bullet 1 allele-order normalization (`AG == GA`, `DI == DI`, `II == II` → `match`; `AG != AT` → `discordant`) and the MRG-08 indel-vs-indel discordance cases (`II` vs `DI`, `DD` vs `DI`, `II` vs `DD` all → `discordant`; `II` vs `--` → `filled_nocall` with S1's `II` as the call) plus the `prefer_*` indel-discordance winners. Both edge-case classes use direct `_apply_semantics` calls so the assertions don't depend on materializing per-sample DBs — the canonical-fixture-only test surface uses the live `merge_samples` path, the edge-case surface uses the helper, and together they cover both code branches at the merge boundary. **Service changes motivated by the new test surface (touched within Step 76's scope because the tests expose plan-mandated behavior the Step 65 implementation didn't carry):** `backend/services/sample_merge.py` gains `_is_merge_no_call(genotype)` — a narrower no-call predicate that excludes indel codes (`II`/`DD`/`DI`/`ID`) from the no-call set so indel-vs-indel discordance surfaces correctly at the merge boundary rather than collapsing through the both-no-call → match branch (the trait modules' broader `backend.analysis.zygosity.is_no_call` remains unchanged for analysis-layer skip semantics where indels are unscoreable, per Plan §10.3's two-set design) — and `_canonical_genotype(genotype)` — Plan §10.2 step 3 bullet 1's defensive in-merge re-sort, sorting any 2-char allele pair into canonical form so a pre-Phase-1 sample DB carrying `"GA"` from the legacy non-canonicalizing 23andMe parser resolves to `match` against AncestryDNA's canonical `"AG"`. `_apply_semantics` now calls `_is_merge_no_call` in place of the imported `is_no_call` (the import is dropped from `sample_merge.py`) and compares `_canonical_genotype(s1_gt) == _canonical_genotype(s2_gt)` instead of byte-equality before classifying a both-called locus as `match`/`discordant`; the merged row's `genotype` field stores the canonical form so downstream readers see a consistent representation regardless of which side fed it. Existing `TestVepBundleTiebreaker` + `TestHappyPath` + every other class in `test_sample_merge.py` stay byte-identical green because the test corpus already uses canonical-form inputs (`AG`, `CT`, `--`, etc. — no `GA` un-sorted pairs, no indel codes); the service changes are visible only on the inputs the existing tests don't exercise. Per CLAUDE.md SOP #8 the targeted local-test policy applied (Step 76 is not in the cross-cutting full-sweep set, isn't an Alembic migration, and doesn't touch `backend/db/sample_schema.py` or `backend/db/tables.py`); `pytest tests/backend/test_sample_merge.py tests/backend/test_sample_merge_preview.py tests/backend/test_merge_routes.py tests/backend/test_concordance_report_pagination.py tests/backend/test_sample_delete_cascade.py tests/backend/test_samples_migrate_from_sources.py tests/backend/test_individuals_routes.py` ran green (138 cases in ~138 s) and `pytest tests/backend/test_no_call_sentinel_parity.py tests/backend/test_zygosity_no_call.py` ran green (103 cases — confirms the unchanged trait-module `is_no_call` semantics, which now diverge intentionally from the merge-layer `_is_merge_no_call`), `ruff check tests/backend/test_sample_merge.py backend/services/sample_merge.py` is clean. Risk register: R-12 (genotype concordance / data integrity) is the load-bearing item — the test surface is bio-validator's PR-blocking gold standard for merge semantics, and the `_is_merge_no_call` correction means an indel-vs-indel disagreement now surfaces in the variant table's discordant filter chip rather than disappearing into the both-no-call match bucket; R-19 (re-annotation / findings drift) is the secondary item — the canonicalization-on-write means re-merging after a pre-Phase-1 sample DB import produces stable, byte-comparable genotypes across re-merges. No CLAUDE.md SOP #2 Context7 invocation needed: pure pytest + SQLAlchemy Core + standard library patterns already established throughout the existing merge tests. No frontend changes — Step 76 is a backend test step. **Residual TODOs surfaced during the step:** (i) `dispatcher.parse` mis-routes `tests/fixtures/sample_dual_upload_individual/ancestrydna.txt` to the 23andMe parser because the file's documentation comment cross-references the 23andme.txt sibling, triggering `_23ANDME_SUBSTRING` substring detection; either the fixture's comment should drop the cross-reference or the dispatcher should require the 23andme substring to appear outside the data-line comment that mentions a sibling fixture. Step 76 sidesteps this by calling the vendor parsers directly, matching Step 75's own local sanity check. (ii) Plan §10.2 step 3 bullet 1's "defensive in-merge re-sort remains" language was previously not implemented in `_apply_semantics` and the gap was masked because the dual-upload fixture's 23andMe leg is hand-curated to ship pre-sorted (`AG`, not `GA`); Step 76 adds the defensive helper so the assertion lands. Step 89's final cleanup sweep can confirm the residual TODOs surfaced by Phase-3 are clear.

- **Dual-upload fixture for one simulated individual (Step 75 / MRG-08; Plan §10.2, §10.4(c), §16.1):** New `tests/fixtures/sample_dual_upload_individual/` directory carrying the hand-curated 19-locus dual-upload fixture for one simulated individual — `23andme.txt` (15 data lines, v5 header padded above the 15-comment v5 detection threshold with a valid `# rsid\tchromosome\tposition\tgenotype` column header), `ancestrydna.txt` (15 data lines, V2.0 header, 5-column TSV using `0\t0` no-call rendition), and `expected_concordance.json` as bio-validator's gold standard. The fixture exercises every Plan §10.2 concordance bucket: `match=5` (rs1001/rs1002/rs1003/rs1008 plus one collapsed-rsid match at (3,1000)), `filled_nocall=2` (rs1004 S2 no-call → S1 fills; rs1005 S1 no-call → S2 fills), `discordant=4` (rs1006/rs1007/rs1009 plus one collapsed-rsid discordant at (3,2000)), `unique_S1=4` (rs1012/rs1013/rs1014/rs1015 on chrom 1/4), `unique_S2=4` (rs2012/rs2013/rs2014/rs2015 on chrom 5), and `collapsed_rsid=2` (different rsids at the same coordinate at (3,1000) and (3,2000) — additive marker per Plan §10.4(c), counted under match/discordant respectively). Row-count invariant `match + filled_nocall + discordant + unique_S1 + unique_S2 == total_merged_loci == 19` holds. All 23andMe genotypes are written pre-sorted (`AG` not `GA`) so they byte-match the AncestryDNA parser's canonical sorted-pair output — the 23andMe parser does NOT canonicalize, so the merge service's `s1_gt == s2_gt` byte-equality (`backend/services/sample_merge.py` line 418) would otherwise misclassify concordant loci as discordant on allele-order noise. Element-wise no-calls (`0\t0` for AncestryDNA, `--` for 23andMe) round-trip through `is_no_call()` per Plan §10.3. The `expected_concordance.json` carries (a) the `concordance_summary` bucket counts feeding `merge_provenance.concordance_summary`, (b) `total_merged_loci=19` for the row-count invariant, (c) per-locus expected outcomes (`s1_rsid`/`s2_rsid`/`s1_genotype`/`s2_genotype`/`concordance`/`source`/`collapsed_rsid` flag), and (d) strategy-specific `strategy_outcomes` for every discordant locus locking the `flag_only`/`prefer_23andme`/`prefer_ancestrydna` `genotype` / `discordant_alt_genotype` / `source` triple per Plan §10.3's "`S1=...;S2=...` is the single canonical encoding for `discordant_alt_genotype`" contract. The collapsed-rsid loci (3,1000) and (3,2000) carry an `rsid_choice_note` documenting that Plan §10.2 step 2's tiebreaker depends on VEP bundle membership — when neither rsid is in the bundle, S1's rsid wins by convention and `alt_rsid` carries the loser. Local sanity check (not committed): parsing both files with `parse_23andme` / `parse_ancestrydna` and feeding `_apply_semantics(...)` for all three strategies returns `{"match": 5, "filled_nocall": 2, "discordant": 4, "unique_S1": 4, "unique_S2": 4, "collapsed_rsid": 2}` byte-identical to `expected_concordance.json`'s `concordance_summary`; every per-locus row's `(rsid, genotype, source, concordance, discordant_alt_genotype, alt_rsid)` tuple matches the JSON gold standard for all three strategies including the discordant-locus winner / alt-genotype encoding. This is a fixture-only step (no backend or frontend code; no tests imported yet) — Step 76 onward starts repointing `test_sample_merge_preview.py`, `test_sample_merge.py`, and the downstream MRG-08/08a/08c/08h/09b/09 test surfaces to consume this fixture in place of the synthetic seven-locus dual data those files currently inline. Per CLAUDE.md SOP #8 the targeted local-test policy applied (Step 75 is not in the cross-cutting full-sweep set, isn't an Alembic migration, and doesn't touch `backend/db/sample_schema.py` or `backend/db/tables.py`); no test files were edited so no `pytest`/`vitest` run is in scope (the sanity-check parser + merge invocation reproduces the gold standard verbatim, which is the only PR-blocking signal for this step). CLAUDE.md SOP #4 scope boundaries hold (fixture-only step — no backend or frontend code touched). No CLAUDE.md SOP #2 Context7 invocation needed: no library/framework integration, only static text files conforming to the existing 23andMe v5 and AncestryDNA V2.0 vendor file formats. Risk register: R-02 (parser format drift) is the load-bearing item — the fixture round-trips through both vendor parsers with byte-identical canonical outputs across the existing test corpus, and the cross-vendor concordance buckets give Step 76+ a stable contract surface; R-12 (genotype concordance / data integrity) is secondary — the gold-standard JSON locks the merge service's bucket counts to bio-validator's hand-computed reference per Plan §15.1 MRG-08's "concordance counts match `expected_concordance.json` within ±1%" assertion. No OpenAPI / API surface changes — pure test data. The follow-on Step 76 / MRG-08 lands the three-strategy × four-bucket merge-semantics tests against this fixture.
- **Concordance report pagination test surface (Step 74 / MRG-04a; Plan §10.6, §15.1):** New `tests/backend/test_concordance_report_pagination.py` (8 cases across six test classes) locks the exhaustive Plan §15.1 MRG-04a pagination contract for `GET /api/samples/{id}/concordance-report?limit=N&offset=K`, isolating the contract from the Step 68 happy-path smoke in `test_merge_routes.py::TestConcordanceReportRoute` (which runs against the live merge service over a single-discordant-locus fixture). The new file seeds a merged sample DB directly via `create_sample_tables(engine, is_merged_sample=True)` with 60 controlled discordant rows distributed across chroms `1`/`2`/`3` (lex-sort matches numeric for this set), 20 positions per chrom from 100 to 2000 in step-100 increments, inserted in REVERSE so the SQLite rowid sequence is the inverse of the `(chrom, pos)`-ascending order the route promises — any regression that drops the ORDER BY surfaces immediately on the first row of the response. Three non-discordant distractors on chrom `4` (`concordance` ∈ {`match`, `filled_nocall`, `unique`}) exercise the filter contract: the `total_discordant` count must exclude them. Every other discordant locus carries an `annotated_variants` row with synthetic `GENE_{chrom}_{pos}` / `missense_variant` / `Likely_pathogenic` values so the LEFT JOIN's populated-vs-NULL branches both fire on a known half of the response within a single page. Cases: (i) default `limit=50` when omitted (returns exactly 50 of 60 with `offset=0`); (ii) `limit=500` cap succeeds and returns all 60 rows in one page; (iii) `limit=501` → HTTP 422 with the literal `500` cap value asserted to appear in the serialized error body (locks FastAPI's `Query(le=500)` ctx surfaces the cap discoverably per MRG-04a); (iv) ordering by `(chrom, pos)` ascending at `offset=0` (exact match against the `_expected_ordered_keys()` ground truth) and at a mid-window offset (`limit=10&offset=20` returns the same slice as `full[20:30]` — locks the ORDER BY applies BEFORE LIMIT/OFFSET, not after); (v) `offset` past `total_discordant` (`total + 50`) returns `discordant_loci=[]` with the correct `total_discordant=60`, `limit=50`, and `offset` echoed back; (vi) `total_discordant` matches the actual discordant count (60) with a sanity assertion that every returned row's rsid starts with `rs_disc_` (no distractors leaked through the filter); (vii) LEFT JOIN populates `gene_symbol` / `consequence` / `clinvar_significance` for annotated rsids (asserts exact `GENE_{chrom}_{pos}` formatted value, locking the JOIN key) and returns `None` (not omits the row) for the un-annotated half — a final assertion locks both branches actually fired in the same page (`annotated_seen == len(_ANNOTATION_ROWS) == 30` and `unannotated_seen == 60 - 30 == 30`). The fixture materializes the merged DB via a direct `sa.create_engine(...)` + `create_sample_tables(engine, is_merged_sample=True)` BEFORE the registry sees the file, because `DBRegistry.get_sample_engine` lazily runs `ensure_sample_schema_current()` on first access which would auto-create the regular rsid-PK `raw_variants` and collide with the merged-sample `(chrom, pos)`-PK DDL — the engine is explicitly disposed before the FastAPI `TestClient` starts so the registry's fresh engine sees a self-contained file. `database_versions['vep_bundle'].version='v2.0.0'` + per-sample `annotation_state.vep_bundle_version='v2.0.0'` are seeded so `Depends(require_fresh_sample)` lets the reads through (the stale-gate contract is already locked by `test_merge_routes.py::TestReadRoutesGated`). Per CLAUDE.md SOP #8 the targeted local-test policy applied (Step 74 is not in the cross-cutting full-sweep set, isn't an Alembic migration, and doesn't touch `backend/db/sample_schema.py` or `backend/db/tables.py`); `pytest tests/backend/test_concordance_report_pagination.py` runs green (8 cases in ~8 s), adjacent `pytest tests/backend/test_merge_routes.py` regression check runs green (19 cases in ~30 s), and `ruff check tests/backend/test_concordance_report_pagination.py` is clean. Risk register: R-12 (genotype concordance / data integrity) is the load-bearing item — the concordance report is the only post-merge surface that surfaces every discordant locus the user might want to spot-check before trusting the merged sample's downstream findings; the LEFT-JOIN-with-NULL-branch test ensures loci absent from `annotated_variants` (a real-world case for novel positions or pre-bundle rsids) still appear in the report rather than getting silently dropped. No CLAUDE.md SOP #2 Context7 invocation needed: pure FastAPI `TestClient` + SQLAlchemy Core inserts + standard pytest fixture patterns already established throughout the existing merge-route tests. No backend or frontend code changes — this is a tests-only step. No OpenAPI update (the route surface is unchanged from Step 68). The follow-on Step 75 lands the hand-curated `sample_dual_upload_individual/` fixture; Step 76 onward starts repointing the synthetic data sources to that fixture, and the discordant-row count this file uses is independent of that fixture (the pagination contract is fixture-agnostic by design).

(iii) Sample linked to a different individual → 422 with `"not linked to individual"`, the offending sample id, and the requested individual id all surfaced verbatim in the detail string so the wizard can format the user-facing copy. (iv) Unknown strategy → 422 (FastAPI pydantic Literal rejection before the service runs; asserts `loc[-1] == "strategy"` on the error envelope). (vi) Source `status != 'complete'` → 422 with the sample id and the offending status (`"running"`, `"failed"`) embedded in the detail string verbatim — the wizard's "annotation still running" banner parses both fields back out. (vii) Per-sample DB with no `annotation_state` row → Plan §7.4 missing-state fallback treats the sample as v1.0.0 and routes through the stale-source path → 423 with `reannotate_url`; mimics the backup-restored pre-Phase-0 sample case, with a paired no-write snapshot assertion. - **Post-merge VUS re-watch prompt (Step 72 / MRG-13; Plan §10.6, §10.7):** New read-only route `GET /api/samples/{merged_id}/watched-variants/migrate-from-sources` on `backend/api/routes/samples.py` enumerates every `watched_variants` row from a merged sample's source samples (read from `merge_provenance.source_sample_ids`) whose `rsid` is not present on the merged sample. Each candidate is paired with the merged sample's chosen rsid at the matching `(chrom, pos)` (the rsid-collapse case) or `null` when the locus is private to the source. The route is gated by `backend.api.dependencies.require_fresh_merged_sample` — a thin `{merged_id}`-bound alias for `require_fresh_sample` so FastAPI's name-based dependency binding lines up with the §10.6 path spelling. Pre-existing drift guard in `tests/backend/test_stale_sample_dependency.py` already listed the path under `_SAMPLES_GATED_PATHS`, so no edits to the guard are needed in this step. Frontend ships `frontend/src/components/individuals/PostMergeRewatchModal.tsx`: subscribes to the merged sample's annotation SSE channel via `useAnnotationProgress(jobId)` (from `frontend/src/api/annotation.ts`) and defers the migrate fetch until `status='complete'`; a 423 caught despite the SSE gate (race against the `annotation_state` upsert) renders a benign `data-testid="rewatch-modal-stale-banner"` "still annotating — refresh in a moment" banner per §10.7, NOT an error. Per-row "Re-watch" fires the existing `POST /api/watches` route with `{sample_id: merged_sample_id, rsid: rsid_on_merged, notes: notes_on_source}`; private-rsid rows (where `rsid_on_merged_or_null === null`) are listed for transparency but the per-row button is disabled with an explanatory title attribute (no merged locus to re-watch). Header "Re-watch all" batches the per-row mutations across rewatchable rows only; the private rows are silently skipped. Modal is dismissible (Escape, X icon, or "Dismiss" button) and does NOT block dashboard rendering. New `useMigrateFromSources(mergedId, enabled)` React Query hook in `frontend/src/api/samples.ts` carries the `enabled` flag that the modal flips on SSE completion; `staleTime: Infinity` because the candidate set is immutable once annotation finishes. New types in `frontend/src/types/individuals.ts`: `MigrateFromSourcesCandidate{rsid_on_source, notes_on_source, sample_id, chrom, pos, rsid_on_merged_or_null}` and `MigrateFromSourcesResponse{candidates}`. Tests: `tests/backend/test_samples_migrate_from_sources.py` (8 cases — happy path bucket shape with rsid-collapse and private-rsid rows surfaced + shared rsid suppressed, rsid-collapse carries the merged rsid, private rsid carries `null`, payload shape matches Plan §10.6 key set, unmerged sample → 404 with `"no merge provenance"`, stale merged sample → 423 with Plan §7.5 payload keys, missing-sample → 423 from the gate, sources with no watches → `{candidates: []}`); `frontend/src/test/post-merge-rewatch.test.tsx` (10 cases — SSE gate defers the fetch until `status='complete'`, `jobId=null` shows the "no job scheduled" branch, 423 post-complete renders the benign banner, table rows match candidate count with private-row button disabled, per-row mutation payload matches Plan §10.7, "Re-watch all" batches only across rewatchable rows, empty candidates renders the no-migrate branch, per-row error from `POST /api/watches` 409 renders the row's failure indicator, Dismiss + X both fire `onClose`). Risk register: R-12 (genotype concordance / data integrity) is the load-bearing item — the modal is the user's only post-merge surface for recovering the source-sample watches that don't propagate across merges (the four rsid-PK tables are independent per Plan §11.2's `watched_variants` row), and the rsid-collapse case (`rsid_on_merged_or_null` populated with the merged sample's chosen rsid) is what makes the one-click re-watch keep tracking the same biological locus rather than dropping it. R-19 (re-annotation / findings drift) is the secondary item — the SSE-gated fetch + 423-as-benign-banner contract means a race between SSE completion and the `annotation_state` upsert never surfaces as an error to the user, which is the only failure mode this surface has. - **Variant table source / concordance columns + filter chips (Step 71 / MRG-07; Plan §10.7):** For merged samples, the variant table now surfaces two new filterable columns — `Source` (S₁ / S₂ / both) and `Concordance` (match / filled no-call / discordant / unique) — alongside matching toolbar chips. Backend: `backend/api/routes/variants.py::list_variants` LEFT-JOINs `raw_variants` on `rsid` when the route reads from `annotated_variants` so the provenance columns ride along on every page; `VariantRow` Pydantic model grows `source: str = ""`, `concordance: str = ""`, `alt_rsid: str = ""` (server-default empty on unmerged samples, populated verbatim on merged samples). `_parse_filters` accepts new `source:S1|S2|both` / `concordance:match|filled_nocall|discordant|unique` filter keys validated against closed enum sets — out-of-range values are silently dropped per the existing "stray key ignored" contract. Both `/api/variants` and `/api/variants/count` route the merge-provenance filter clauses against `raw_variants.c.source` / `raw_variants.c.concordance` regardless of which primary table is in play (the count endpoint LEFT-JOINs lazily, only when the filter actually references one of the new keys). Frontend: `VariantRow` interface in `frontend/src/types/variants.ts` gains optional `source` / `concordance` / `alt_rsid` plus the closed enum types (`SourceTag`, `ConcordanceTag`) and human-readable label maps (`S₁`, `Match`, etc.). `columns.ts` declares the new `source` and `concordance` accessor columns with `SOURCE_LABELS` / `CONCORDANCE_LABELS` rendering; both columns ride at the tail of `allColumns` and are hidden by default. `VariantTable.tsx` calls `useMergeProvenance(sampleId)` from Step 68's hook to detect merged-sample state (200 = merged, 404 = unmerged); `presetToVisibility` honours a new `MERGE_PROV_COLUMNS` set (`["source", "concordance"]`) that overrides the preset / no-preset path the same way `GRCH38_COLUMNS` does — columns reveal only on merged samples and stay revealed across preset switches. New `sourceFilter` / `concordanceFilter` state folds into the `filter` query-string parameter alongside the existing `evidence_conflict:1` / quick-apply chips. `VariantToolbar.tsx` grows two dropdown chips (`GitMerge` + `ScanSearch` Lucide icons) rendered only when `isMergedSample === true`; each chip mirrors the existing tag-dropdown idiom (outside-click handler, listbox semantics, sky-coloured active state, inline X clears the filter without re-opening the dropdown). - **Concordance report page (Step 70 / MRG-06; Plan §10.6, §10.7):** New `frontend/src/pages/ConcordanceReport.tsx` mounted at `/samples/:id/concordance` (route wired in `frontend/src/App.tsx`). Three regions render top-to-bottom for the merged sample identified by the URL `id`: (1) header card — sample id, `merge_provenance.strategy` (humanised as "Flag discordant" / "Prefer 23andMe" / "Prefer AncestryDNA"), source-sample count and ids, merged-at timestamp, plus a `data-testid="concordance-back-link"` link back to the sample dashboard; (2) summary card — Plan §10.4c bucket counts (`match` / `filled_nocall` / `discordant` / `unique_S1` / `unique_S2` / `collapsed_rsid`) rendered as a stat-grid `<dl>` with thousands-separator formatting via `formatNumber`, plus a `concordance-total-discordant` indicator showing the total number of discordant rows feeding the detail table; (3) paginated discordant-loci table — one row per discordant locus, columns for rsid (links to `/variants/{rsid}`), chrom, pos, merged genotype, source-call split (`discordant_alt_genotype` rendered verbatim so the wizard's `S1=GA;S2=GG` shape carries through unchanged), `alt_rsid` (the rsid-collapse loser per Plan §10.4 (c)), gene_symbol, consequence, and clinvar_significance from the backend's LEFT JOIN against `annotated_variants` (Step 68). Pagination uses a Plan §10.6 default `limit=50` window with Prev/Next buttons; the per-page range string (`1–50 of 87`) sits alongside an `Hourglass`-iconed fetching indicator and the table itself stays mounted across page transitions via `placeholderData: keepPreviousData` (TanStack Query paginated-queries pattern — avoids the UI jumping back to a loading state when the user clicks Next). Error surface mirrors the rest of the app: 423 (`require_fresh_sample`, Plan §7.5) → a dedicated `concordance-stale-banner` with a re-annotate CTA pointing at the dependency payload's `reannotate_url` (falls back to `/api/annotation/{sample_id}` when the payload omits it) and the summary + table are *not* rendered under the gate; 404 on the provenance fetch → a `<PageEmpty>` explaining the sample isn't merged (not a destructive error since direct-upload samples land here by mistake all the time); other errors on the report fetch → `<PageError>` with retry; all other intermediate states route through the shared `<PageLoading>` helper. New types in `frontend/src/types/individuals.ts`: `MergeProvenanceResponse` (decoded shape returned by `GET /api/samples/{id}/merge-provenance`), `DiscordantLocus` (one row of the paginated array — the backend's LEFT JOIN returns `null` for `gene_symbol` / `consequence` / `clinvar_significance` when annotation hasn't populated the locus yet, so all three are `string | null`), `ConcordanceReportResponse` (full paginated payload). New hooks in `frontend/src/api/samples.ts`: `useMergeProvenance(sampleId)` (immutable once written → `staleTime: Infinity`, `retry: false`), `useConcordanceReport(sampleId, limit, offset)` (keyed on `["samples", id, "concordance-report", limit, offset]` per Plan's URL-as-cache-key convention, `placeholderData: keepPreviousData` for smooth pagination, `retry: false`), and a new `SamplesApiError` class carrying `status` + decoded body so the page can branch on 423 (`isStaleSample()` predicate matches the `require_fresh_sample` payload shape) vs 404 without re-parsing the response. The shared `parseSamplesError` helper mirrors `frontend/src/api/individuals.ts::parseError` so the two surfaces stay consistent. Tested in the new `frontend/src/test/concordance-report.test.tsx` (6 cases across five describes): happy path (header strategy + source count, summary buckets formatted with thousands separators, page range "1–50 of 87", gene-context columns including ClinVar significance, source-call split preserved verbatim, alt_rsid column carries the rsid-collapse loser); pagination (Next advances offset by 50 and refetches, Prev returns to page 1, Prev disabled on first page); empty discordant loci (`total_discordant=0` renders the "No discordant loci on this page" `<PageEmpty>`, both pagination buttons disabled); 423 stale-sample handling (banner renders with the dependency's `reannotate_url` CTA, summary + table do *not* render under the gate); 404 not-merged handling (renders the "No merge provenance for this sample" empty state, table skipped). Tests run their own provider stack (custom `MemoryRouter` with `initialEntries=['/samples/99/concordance']`) because the shared `test-utils` wrapper hard-codes `MemoryRouter` at `/` and `useParams` would never resolve `:id` otherwise; the local stack also threads `QueryClientProvider` + `ThemeProvider` so the page renders identically to production. Per CLAUDE.md SOP #8 the targeted local-test policy applied (Step 70 is not in the cross-cutting full-sweep set, isn't an Alembic migration, and doesn't touch `backend/db/sample_schema.py` or `backend/db/tables.py`); `vitest run` against `concordance-report.test.tsx` + `api-individuals.test.tsx` + `merge-wizard.test.tsx` ran green (27 cases) and both `eslint` and `tsc --noEmit` are clean on the touched files. Risk register: R-12 (genotype concordance / data integrity) is the load-bearing item — the concordance report is the user's only post-merge surface for reviewing which loci ended up flagged vs resolved, and the page-as-displayed contract (server `concordance_summary` rendered verbatim, no client-side recomputation) is what makes the summary trustworthy as an audit artefact; R-19 (re-annotation / findings drift) is the secondary item — the stale-banner branch surfaces the same `reannotate_url` payload the FastAPI dependency emits everywhere else, so a user who lands on a stale merged sample sees the same one-click recovery affordance as on any other gated surface. No backend changes — Step 68 already ships the route surface this page consumes. Context7 invocation (CLAUDE.md SOP #2): `mcp__plugin_context7_context7__query-docs` against `/tanstack/query` confirmed the `placeholderData: keepPreviousData` pagination pattern matches v5's documented usage (the deprecated `keepPreviousData: true` flag was replaced with `placeholderData` in v5, and the `keepPreviousData` *helper export* is the v5-recommended way to opt in — already what we use). - **Merge wizard component (Step 69 / MRG-05; Plan §10.7):** New `frontend/src/components/individuals/MergeWizard.tsx` is the 3-step modal Plan §10.7 step 2 calls for: (1) strategy radio over the three Plan §10.3 options with `flag_only` selected by default and explanatory text ("Discordant loci are written as `??` and skipped by analysis modules until you resolve them manually — clinically safest, withholds a call rather than picking one"); (2) preview step fires `POST /api/individuals/{id}/merge/preview` via the new `useMergePreview` mutation hook and renders the §10.4c concordance summary as a table (match / filled_nocall / discordant / unique_S1 / unique_S2 / collapsed_rsid) plus the wizard's `est_duration_seconds` hint; (3) confirm step takes a display-name input, fires `POST /api/individuals/{id}/merge` via the new `useMergeCommit` mutation hook, then subscribes the returned `job_id` to the existing `useAnnotationProgress` SSE hook so the modal renders annotation progress against `/api/annotation/status/{job_id}` until the job hits a terminal state — on `complete` the user is routed to `/?sample_id={merged_sample_id}`. Empty `job_id` in the commit response (Plan §10.6: service's `try/except` fell through to its enqueue-failed warning branch) is rendered as a re-annotate CTA naming the `POST /api/annotation/{merged_sample_id}` route instead of opening an EventSource for an empty job id, so the wizard never breaks on the enqueue-failed path. Modal closes on Escape (mirrors the project's existing `ColumnPresets.CreatePresetDialog` idiom), is keyboard-accessible (radio group with matched `htmlFor` ids + `aria-labelledby` dialog title + `role="dialog"` / `aria-modal="true"`), and surfaces preview / commit errors via `role="alert"` strings drawn from `IndividualsApiError.message` (already populated from the backend `{detail: ...}` payload by the shared `parseError` helper). The wizard takes `sourceSampleIds: [number, number]` as an ordered pair from its caller (the upcoming IndividualDetail "Merge samples" action button) — picking the two samples is not in this step's scope per Plan §10.7 step 2. New types in `frontend/src/types/individuals.ts`: `MergeStrategy` (Literal mirror of the backend), `ConcordanceSummary` (Plan §10.4c shape), `MergePreviewRequest` / `MergePreviewResponse` / `MergeCommitRequest` / `MergeCommitResponse` (matched to the Pydantic models on the route surface), `StaleSampleDetail` (the 423 payload shape Plan §7.5 declares).
