- **React Query hooks for `/api/individuals` (Step 48 / IND-04; Plan §9.5):** New `frontend/src/api/individuals.ts` exposes seven hooks (`useIndividuals`, `useIndividual`, `useCreateIndividual`, `useUpdateIndividual`, `useDeleteIndividual`, `useLinkSample`, `useUnlinkSample`) over the Step 47 backend routes. Cache keys are stable per URL param via `individualsKeys.list()` / `individualsKeys.detail(id)`; create/update mutations seed the detail cache, delete removes it; every link/unlink mutation invalidates both the individuals list, the parent detail key, and `["samples"]` + `["samples", sampleId]` so the two-level sample-selector and `<SampleMetadataEditor>` re-render against the new `samples.individual_id` value. Non-2xx responses raise `IndividualsApiError(status, message, body)` with an `isLinkConflict()` predicate that surfaces the Plan §9.3 409 link-conflict body (`sample_id`, `individual_id`, `individual_display_name`, `message`) to consumers without parsing. Shared types land in `frontend/src/types/individuals.ts`. Tested in `frontend/src/test/api-individuals.test.tsx` (11 cases): cache-key stability + null-id branch, list/detail happy paths, list 5xx → typed error, create/update/delete/link/unlink request shape + cache invalidation surface, link-conflict 409 body preservation, `useIndividual(null)` stays disabled with no fetch. Wires the data layer for Steps 49 (two-level sample selector), 50 (`/individuals/{id}` page), and 51 (settings assign-to-individual dropdown).
- **`/api/individuals` routes (Step 47 / IND-03; Plan §9.2, §9.3):** New `backend/api/routes/individuals.py` exposes the seven routes that drive Phase 2's two-level sample selector and `/individuals/{id}` page — `GET /api/individuals` (list with `sample_count`, `vendors[]`, `last_activity`), `POST /api/individuals` (create from `{display_name, notes?, biological_sex?}`), `GET /api/individuals/{id}` (detail + `linked_samples[]` + `aggregated_findings_count` deduped by rsid across linked sample DBs at evidence_level ≥ 3), `PATCH /api/individuals/{id}` (edit fields; empty body → 422), `DELETE /api/individuals/{id}` (explicit `UPDATE samples SET individual_id = NULL` then row delete — independent of SQLite's `PRAGMA foreign_keys`, so the SET-NULL contract from Plan §9.2 holds in every environment; no sample row or per-sample DB file is touched), `POST /api/individuals/{id}/link-sample` (409 with `{sample_id, individual_id, individual_display_name, message}` when the sample is already linked elsewhere; re-linking to the same individual is a no-op), and `POST /api/individuals/{id}/unlink-sample` (422 when the sample is linked to a different individual, no-op when already unlinked). Registered in `backend/main.py`. Tested in `tests/backend/test_individuals_routes.py` (11 cases): happy paths across all seven endpoints + minimal-body create + empty-body / nonexistent 404/422 negatives; 409-on-double-link payload assertion; FK-SET-NULL on individual delete (sample rows survive with `individual_id IS NULL`, per-sample DB files untouched). Remaining IND-09 edge cases (link-elsewhere, nonexistent, aggregated dedup) land in Step 55.
- **`individuals` table + migration 009 (Step 46 / IND-01 + IND-02; Plan §9.2):** New `individuals` reference-DB table (`id`, `display_name`, `notes`, `biological_sex`, `created_at`, `updated_at`) groups one or more `samples` rows under a single biological subject — the foundation for Phase 2 dual-upload aggregation (23andMe + AncestryDNA from the same person). `alembic/versions/009_add_individuals_table.py` (forward-only, sequenced after `008`) creates the table, adds a nullable `samples.individual_id` column with `FOREIGN KEY(individual_id) REFERENCES individuals(id) ON DELETE SET NULL`, and `ix_samples_individual_id` for the two-level sample-selector lookup. SQLite ALTER limitations are worked around via `batch_alter_table` with a named FK constraint (`fk_samples_individual_id`). Pre-009 sample rows surface as `individual_id IS NULL` ("Unassigned" group in the UI). Round-trip tested in `tests/backend/test_alembic_backfill.py::TestMigration009Individuals` (10 cases: table shape, column types, FK target + on-delete clause, index creation, `SET NULL` cascade fires on individual delete, legacy samples remain NULL, downgrade drops everything, upgrade→downgrade→upgrade leaves a known-good shape, head→head idempotency).
- **Phase 1 frontend unit tests (Step 45 / ADNA-12; Plan §13.1):** Explicit AncestryDNA-accept coverage on `<UploadStep>` in `frontend/src/test/setup-upload-step.test.tsx` — file-picker accept for `AncestryDNA.txt` / `.tsv` / `.csv`, drag-and-drop accept, `multipart/form-data` POST shape to `/api/ingest` with the file payload preserved, and the success card rendering `ancestrydna_v2.0` with no bundle-gate banner. New SetupWizard-chrome contract in `frontend/src/test/setup-wizard.test.tsx` — the stepper continues to expose the `Upload` step (terminal AncestryDNA entry point) after `disclaimer_accepted` advances state past step 0, and the existing UploadStep block gains an explicit `ancestrydna_v2.0` happy-path assertion. Closes Phase 1's frontend unit-test budget; the wizard-level walk + ingest is exercised end-to-end by the Playwright spec from Step 44.
- **Setup-wizard AncestryDNA E2E (Step 44 / ADNA-11; Plan §13.1):** `tests/e2e/setup-wizard-ancestrydna.spec.ts` drives the full first-run wizard against a mocked backend in two scenarios. (1) Happy path — bundle v2.0.0 installed, `POST /api/ingest` returns 202 with `file_format="ancestrydna_v2.0"`, the user lands on the Dashboard with `needs_setup=false`. (2) Bundle-gate path — pre-v2.0.0 bundle, the first ingest returns the Plan §5.4 409 `bundle_version_too_old` payload, the in-wizard banner renders with installed + required versions and the ~MB size hint, the update CTA fires `POST /api/updates/trigger` for `vep_bundle`, the polled job resolves `complete`, and the user's retry upload succeeds with 202. Patterned after `setup-wizard-lai.spec.ts`; deterministic across Chromium / Firefox / WebKit via `page.route()` mocks (no real ingest pipeline, no ~600 MB bundle download).
- **Ingest API AncestryDNA happy-path test (Step 43 / ADNA-10; Plan §13.1):** `tests/backend/test_ingestion_api.py::TestIngestAncestryDNA` POSTs `tests/fixtures/sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` to `/api/ingest` against a TestClient seeded with `database_versions['vep_bundle'] = v2.0.0` (new `_seed_vep_bundle_v2` helper + `ancestrydna_client` fixture) and asserts 202 status, `file_format == "ancestrydna_v2.0"`, and `variant_count == 589`. Paired with the 409-gated cases in `test_bundle_gating.py` (Step 7); together they pin both legs of the Plan §5.4 vendor-scoped bundle gate.
- **Nightly slow-tier workflow (Step 42 / ADNA-09a):** `.github/workflows/nightly.yml` runs `pytest -m slow` at 04:00 UTC daily, caches the production VEP + LAI release assets by manifest `sha256`, and auto-files a GitHub Issue labeled `slow-tier-regression` on failure.
- **AncestryDNA real-bundle accuracy test (Step 42):** `tests/backend/test_annotation_engine_ancestrydna_real_bundle.py` asserts ≥95% combined VEP hit-rate and ≥85% ClinVar P/LP hit-rate against the real `vep_bundle v2.0.0` over `synthetic_eur_ancestrydna.txt`. Dormant on PR-blocking runs; activates only inside the nightly workflow.
- **VEP-bundle gate in `requires_real_bundle`:** `tests/conftest.py` now treats either the production LAI or VEP bundle as sufficient to wake the marker, with each test individually skipping if its specific bundle is missing.
- **Ancestry Module v2 (AMv2):** Two-tier ancestry analysis system replacing the 128-AIM IDW approach.
  - **Tier 1 (Instant):** 5,000-AIM PCA projection with NNLS + kNN admixture estimation. Runs in < 1 second.
  - **Tier 2 (Deep Analysis):** Local ancestry inference via re-exported Gnomix models with Beagle phasing. Chromosome-level ancestry painting. Runs in ~15-30 minutes. Optional.
- 7 superpopulations (AFR, AMR, CSA, EAS, EUR, MID, OCE) — up from 6 (SAS renamed to CSA, MID added).
- NPZ-based PCA bundle (414 KB) with 5,000 AIMs, 8 significant PCs, and rsID matching for 23andMe compatibility.
- NNLS admixture with bootstrap 95% confidence intervals (100 iterations).
- kNN secondary admixture estimate with cosine-similarity confidence scoring.
- LAI bundle (~500 MB) hosted on GitHub Releases with resumable download and SHA-256 verification.
- Gnomix inference engine (`gnomix_inference.py`) — pure numpy + XGBoost, no sklearn/pandas dependency.
- LAI runner with pysam-based VCF handling (replaces bcftools/bgzip/tabix subprocess calls).
- Chromosome painting visualization using react-konva (Canvas) with hover tooltips and population legend.
- LAI-derived global ancestry pie chart alongside Tier 1 bar chart.
- Tier 1 vs Tier 2 concordance comparison section.
- Per-population MID accuracy warning when proportion < 15%.
- PCA scatter plot with PC selector dropdown (PC1 vs PC2, PC1 vs PC3, etc.).
- Analysis Details collapsible section with AIM count, PCs used, and method description.
- PRS ancestry mismatch integration: admixture-aware threshold warns when top ancestry < 70%.
- LAI API endpoints: status, trigger, results, and SSE progress.
- LAI results table in sample DB with findings integration.
- Huey task for background LAI processing with job progress tracking.
- Java runtime detection for LAI bundle requirements.
- Setup wizard LAI bundle checkbox (optional, default unchecked).
- "Download LAI Bundle" button on Ancestry page for post-setup download.
- LAI progress UI with per-chromosome phasing and inference status.
- `docs/ANCESTRY_MODULE.md` — methods, validation, limitations, and citations.

### Changed

- Ancestry engine rewritten from IDW-based to NNLS + kNN admixture estimation.
- PCA bundle migrated from JSON to NPZ format (128 AIMs to 5,000 AIMs).
- `get_inferred_ancestry()` consolidated into `ancestry.py` (removed duplicate from `prs.py`).
- `get_inferred_ancestry()` preference order: `local_ancestry` > `nnls_admixture` > `pca_projection`.
- Admixture bar chart updated for 7 populations with percentage labels and confidence badges.
- `POPULATIONS` constant updated from 6 to 7 populations across backend.

### Dependencies

- Added `scipy` (NNLS admixture via `scipy.optimize.nnls`).
- Added `pysam` (VCF read/write, replaces bcftools/bgzip/tabix subprocess calls).
- Added `xgboost` (Gnomix smoother step, loads native-format boosters).
- Added `react-konva` and `konva` (chromosome painting Canvas visualization).

## Setup Wizard ↔ Update Manager Wiring

### PR1 — Manifest, bundle wiring, auto-update endpoint, wizard UX

#### Added

- `bundles/manifest.json` — single manifest pinning bundle versions, SHA-256s, and sizes for `lai_bundle`, `vep_bundle`, `ancestry_pca`, plus upstream URLs and last-known versions for every pipeline DB (`clinvar`, `gnomad`, `dbnsfp`, `cpic`, `gwas_catalog`, `dbsnp`, `mondo_hpo`).
- `backend/db/manifest.py` — frozen dataclasses (`Manifest`, `BundleManifestEntry`, `PipelinePinEntry`) plus `fetch_manifest()` with a 1 h in-memory TTL cache, network-failure fallback to last-good, and a `GENOMEINSIGHT_MANIFEST_PATH` env var override for tests.
- `_record_db_version(engine, db_name, version, file_size_bytes, sha256=None, file_path=None)` — single helper in `backend/db/database_registry.py` that upserts into `database_versions` for every successful build/download path (LAI extraction, ENCODE cCREs build, ClinVar/gnomAD/dbNSFP/CPIC/GWAS/MONDO+HPO/dbSNP).
- LAI extraction now records its row using the manifest's version/SHA-256 (falls back to `unknown-pre-manifest` when the manifest is unreachable).
- `auto_update_settings` table (`db_name PK`, `enabled`, `updated_at`) in `backend/db/tables.py`.
- Alembic migration `007_add_auto_update_settings` — idempotent table creation, seeds `AUTO_UPDATE_DEFAULTS`, and backfills `database_versions("unknown-pre-manifest")` for `lai_bundle`/`encode_ccres` installs that pre-date version tracking.
- `get_auto_update` / `set_auto_update` helpers in `backend/db/update_manager.py`, with fallback to `AUTO_UPDATE_DEFAULTS` for missing rows.
- `POST /api/updates/auto-update` endpoint persisting per-DB toggles (404s for unknown DBs); `GET /api/updates/status` now reads `auto_update` from the table.
- Setup wizard per-DB checkboxes with a running "Total: X.X GB selected" total. Required DBs are checked-and-disabled; `lai_bundle` and `encode_ccres` default checked; `bundled` DBs render as "Included" (no checkbox). The button is now "Download Selected".
- Sonner toast on Continue lists any optional DBs the user skipped, with a pointer to Settings > Update Manager.

#### Changed

- `lai_bundle` `DatabaseInfo` now carries `sha256="959ed0fd…"` as a hardcoded integrity fallback; manifest override applies at download time.
- `backend/api/routes/databases.py` injects manifest URL/SHA-256/size when `db_info.sha256 is None` (download mode); falls back to registry defaults when the manifest is unreachable.
- Per-module `record_*_version` helpers in `clinvar/gnomad/dbnsfp/cpic/gwas/mondo_hpo/dbsnp.py` now delegate to `_record_db_version` (behavior preserved, `file_path` plumbed through).
- `update_manager._record_version` is now a thin pass-through to `_record_db_version` to remove the near-duplicate.

### PR2 — Pipeline DB version checks + scheduler integration

#### Added

- `CHECK_FNS` dispatch dict in `backend/db/update_manager.py` covering every DB.
- Manifest-driven `check_lai_bundle_update` and `check_ancestry_pca_update`.
- Per-pipeline checkers: `check_gnomad_update`, `check_dbnsfp_update`, `check_cpic_update`, `check_gwas_update`, `check_dbsnp_update`, `check_mondo_hpo_update`. Each returns `None` on network error (no spurious banners) and compares the manifest's pinned URL/version against `database_versions`.
- `run_lai_bundle_update` and `run_ancestry_pca_bundle_update` — manifest-driven `DownloadManager` flows that record both `database_versions` and `update_history`.

#### Changed

- `run_vep_bundle_update` now also writes `_record_db_version` + `_record_update_history`, so VEP updates show up in the history log.
- `check_all_updates` refactored to loop `CHECK_FNS` rather than hardcoded ClinVar/VEP branches.
- `run_scheduled_update_check` dispatches across all DBs: respects `get_auto_update`, defers when outside `update_download_window` for ≥100 MB, and routes bundles vs. pipelines correctly.

### PR3 — UI polish, app-update banner, Playwright E2E

#### Added

- `AppUpdateBanner` component on the Dashboard, reading `useAppUpdate()`. Dismissible per-version via `localStorage["appUpdateDismissed"]`.
- UpdateManager top-row "GenomeInsight" entry showing app version and a release-notes link via `useAppUpdate`.
- Bundle rows in UpdateManager now display `v1.1 · 2026-04-07`-style build dates from `version_display`.
- "Update now" outside-window tooltip plus a "Force update" mini-button with a confirm dialog (backend `POST /api/updates/trigger` accepts `force=true`).
- Playwright E2E: `tests/e2e/setup-wizard-lai.spec.ts` exercises the wizard with the LAI checkbox; `tests/e2e/update-manager-lai.spec.ts` clicks "Update now" on a preloaded `unknown-pre-manifest` LAI and asserts new `database_versions` + `update_history` rows.

#### Changed

- Removed the obsolete "Run scripts/build_vep_bundle.py" hint from `DatabasesStep.tsx` — VEP updates now flow through the manifest.

## AncestryDNA Integration

### Phase 1 — AncestryDNA Single-Sample Ingestion

#### Step 40 — PR-blocking annotation pipeline regression test

**Files touched**

- `backend/annotation/engine.py` (modified; ADNA-09; Plan §5.1, §5.6) — wired the VEP `(chrom, pos)` coordinate-fallback path into `run_annotation`. Added `AnnotationEngineResult.vep_coord_fallback_matched: int = 0` to record the subset of `vep_matched` that resolved via coordinate lookup, and a new private helper `_vep_coord_fallback(batch_rsids, raw_by_rsid, vep_engine, vep_data, result)` that runs *after* the concurrent rsid/ClinVar/gnomAD/dbNSFP futures complete (so gene-phenotype lookup sees the augmented `vep_data`). The helper delegates to the existing `backend.annotation.vep_bundle.lookup_vep_by_positions`, mutates `vep_data` in place with any coord matches (keyed by the sample rsid, not the bundle rsid), and folds coord-fallback wall-clock time onto `result.timing_vep_s` so the existing P4-22 timing accounting stays single-source. The `_build_coverage_stats` call site now passes real per-bucket counts — `vep_rsid_hits = result.vep_matched - result.vep_coord_fallback_matched`, `vep_coord_fallback_hits = result.vep_coord_fallback_matched` — replacing the previous hardcoded `vep_coord_fallback_hits=0` reservation. The Plan §5.6 telemetry payload now reports both buckets independently; rollup math is unchanged because `vep_matched` still aggregates both paths so `vep_misses = total - vep_matched` continues to hold.
- `tests/backend/test_annotation_engine_ancestrydna.py` (new file; ADNA-09; Plan §13.1, §5.1, §5.6) — `TestAncestryDNAAnnotationPipeline` locks the three ADNA-09 contracts against the AncestryDNA fixture:
  - `test_hit_rate_and_coord_fallback` parses `tests/fixtures/sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` via the production `backend.ingestion.dispatcher.parse`, loads the 589 parsed variants into an in-memory per-sample DB with `file_format="ancestrydna_v2.0"`, runs `run_annotation` against an in-memory VEP bundle seeded from `tests/fixtures/seed_csvs/vep_seed.csv` (the same source the regenerated mini bundle is built from) augmented with two coord-fallback rows at `(chrom=1, pos=2000000)` and `(chrom=2, pos=3000000)` — the fixture coordinates of the defensive `kgp12345678` / `kgp98765432` rows that step 39 deliberately omitted by rsid. Asserts `rsid_hits / total >= 1 - kgp_count/total` (the rsID hit-rate floor specified in Plan §13.1), `coord_fallback_hits >= kgp_count` (the kgp rows resolve via the (chrom, pos) path), `rsid_hits + coord_fallback_hits == total` (combined VEP coverage hits every fixture row), and `vep_misses == 0`.
  - `test_annotation_coverage_bitmask_propagation` re-runs the engine and asserts every persisted `annotated_variants` row carries the `VEP_BIT` (the AncestryDNA pipeline must propagate the bitmask), and that the count of bit-set rows equals `result.rows_written` — no quiet drop between merge and upsert.
  - `test_telemetry_shape` asserts the Plan §5.6 payload: `coverage_stats["bundle_version"] == "v2.0.0"`, `list(by_source.keys()) == ["ancestrydna"]` (single-key lowercase derivation from `file_format` for unmerged samples), the per-source value-dict carries exactly the three required keys (`vep_bundle_rsid_hits`, `vep_bundle_coord_fallback_hits`, `vep_misses`), and per-source counts sum to `total_variants`.
- `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry).

**Decisions**

- **Coord-fallback wiring lives in the engine, not in `_lookup_vep`.** The four concurrent annotation-source adapters (`_lookup_vep`, `_lookup_clinvar`, `_lookup_gnomad`, `_lookup_dbnsfp`) each return a plain `dict[str, dict]`; adding internal coord-fallback to `_lookup_vep` would either change its return signature (breaking `TestLookupVep` and other consumers) or hide the rsid-vs-coord distinction the Plan §5.6 telemetry requires. The cleanest factoring mirrors how `_lookup_gene_phenotype` is already plumbed: run the new helper sequentially in the per-batch loop *after* `as_completed` populates `vep_data`, then continue into gene-phenotype lookup so it sees both rsid and coord-matched VEP rows. `_lookup_gnomad` / `_lookup_dbnsfp` already use raw_by_rsid for their own coord fallbacks; the `_lookup_vep` adapter accepted `raw_by_rsid` as an unused parameter and now stays consistent with that interface while the coord-fallback step uses it in the caller.
- **The in-memory bundle, not the on-disk `mini_vep_bundle.db`.** Step 40's spec reads "using the regenerated mini bundle"; the test file uses the same `vep_seed.csv` source the regen script consumes (so it cannot drift from the mini bundle's rsID coverage) and adds two extra rows at the exact `(chrom, pos)` of the fixture's kgp\* entries. This is the same in-memory pattern `test_annotation_engine.py::vep_engine_inmemory` already uses for the existing coverage_stats tests; introducing a separate on-disk-bundle path in the new file would require either a writable copy of `mini_vep_bundle.db` or a temp-dir regenerate-on-fixture-startup step, neither of which step 40 mandates. The two coord-fallback rows carry the `rs_coord_fallback_{0,1}` rsIDs (deliberately non-`kgp*`) and a placeholder `FIXTURE_GENE` / `intron_variant` payload — sufficient for the bitmask + telemetry-shape assertions; the per-row annotation content is not inspected.
- **gnomAD / dbNSFP intentionally left unavailable in the fixture.** The ADNA-09 contract is VEP-bundle hit-rate; the mock registry's `gnomad_engine` / `dbnsfp_engine` properties raise `RuntimeError` so the engine takes the `_check_engine_available → None` branch for each, exercising the graceful-degradation path on a fresh AncestryDNA install where the optional databases have not yet been downloaded. The engine still emits the full coverage_stats payload because that path runs unconditionally at the end of `run_annotation`.
- **`AnnotationEngineResult.vep_matched` keeps its existing semantics — total VEP hits across both buckets.** Adding `vep_coord_fallback_matched` as a *subset* counter rather than a peer keeps every existing consumer (`TestCoverageStatsPayload`, the structured-log line, `result.total_matched`) byte-identical for the all-rsid case. The `_build_coverage_stats` call subtracts the subset to compute the rsid-only count for the payload.

**Scope discipline (per the per-step PR convention)**

- Only `backend/annotation/engine.py`, the new test file, and `CHANGELOG.md` are touched. The `vep_seed.csv` and on-disk `mini_vep_bundle.db` are not modified — the coord-fallback bundle rows live exclusively in the test fixture's in-memory engine. No frontend, parser, dispatcher, ingestion, or schema surface changes. The Plan §5.1 description of the coord-fallback as "preserved as defense-in-depth — `kgp*` / internal IDs with a known coordinate but no rsid mapping resolve here" is now actually implemented in the engine; previously it was reserved at `0` with a TODO comment, so step 40 closes the rsid-side gap that step 9 deferred when it landed the telemetry payload shape.

**Test sweep (CLAUDE.md SOP #8)**

- Step 40 is not on the canonical full-sweep list (full-sweep set: 8, 13, 17, 29, 46, 54, 61, 62, 63, 64, 65, 66; phase boundaries: 18, 19, 45, 59, 87). It touches one production module and one new test file — no migrations, no per-sample schema declarations, no shared fixtures. Targeted local sweep: `pytest tests/backend/test_annotation_engine_ancestrydna.py tests/backend/test_annotation_engine.py` — 86 cases green (83 pre-step-40 + 3 new). Companion sweep of every other importer of `backend.annotation.engine`: `pytest tests/backend/test_huey_annotation.py tests/backend/test_admin_api.py tests/backend/test_performance_optimization.py tests/backend/test_benchmark.py` — all still green; no consumer relied on `vep_coord_fallback_hits` staying at zero. Ruff clean on the two touched files.

**Risk-register touch points (Plan §1.3)**

- **R-04** (annotation pipeline correctness) — the AncestryDNA-sourced sample DB now has a PR-blocking regression test that locks the rsID hit-rate floor, the coord-fallback path for `kgp*` / internal IDs, the `annotation_coverage` bitmask propagation, and the Plan §5.6 telemetry shape against a deterministic fixture. The engine's previous "VEP currently has no coord fallback; reserve the field at 0" reservation is replaced with a real implementation that mirrors the gnomAD / dbNSFP path; the per-bucket counts in `coverage_stats` now reflect actual lookup behaviour rather than a hardcoded zero. **R-19** (test-fixture provenance) — the in-memory VEP bundle is seeded from the already-committed `vep_seed.csv` plus two coord-fallback rows synthesized from the already-committed `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` `kgp*` coordinates; no consultation of the local-only real export, no real user genotypes. The placeholder synthetic annotation payload on the two coord-fallback rows is not user-facing data and only exists inside the test process.

---

#### Step 39 — Regenerate mini VEP bundle for AncestryDNA coverage

##### Added

- `tests/fixtures/seed_csvs/vep_seed.csv` (extended) — appends 579 new `vep_annotations` rows so the mini VEP bundle deterministically covers every non-`kgp*` rsID in `tests/fixtures/sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` (ADNA-09 prerequisite; Plan §16.1). Each new row carries the rsID and the fixture's coordinate after the Plan §8.4 AncestryDNA chromosome normalization (`23→X`, `24→Y`, `25→X` for PAR collapse, `26→MT`). Ref/alt are derived deterministically from the fixture's `allele1`/`allele2` pair: heterozygous nucleotides → alphabetical `(min,max)`; homozygous nucleotides → `(allele, complementary)` via `A↔G`/`C↔T`; no-call (`0`) → `A/G` fallback after using any present nucleotide; indels → `I/D`. The remaining columns are placeholder synthetic values (`gene_symbol=""`, `transcript_id=""`, `consequence="intron_variant"`, `strand="+"`, `mane_select=0`) since step 39's contract is presence-in-bundle for rsID hits, not annotation realism. The 8 fixture rsIDs already present in the seed (`rs429358`, `rs7412`, `rs1801133`, `rs1801131`, `rs4244285`, `rs334`, `rs16947`, `rs3892097`) are preserved verbatim — their existing real-world annotations are kept rather than overwritten with synthetic rows.
- `tests/fixtures/mini_vep_bundle.db` (regenerated) — rebuilt from the extended seed via `python scripts/regenerate_fixtures.py` (no script changes); now carries 679 `vep_annotations` rows (up from 100), with `bundle_metadata.variant_count = "679"` and the existing `bundle_version = "v2.0.0"` / `schema_version = "1"` / `ensembl_version = "112"` Phase 0 metadata block intact.
- `tests/backend/test_regenerate_fixtures.py::TestRegenerateFixtures::test_mini_vep_bundle_covers_ancestrydna_rsids` (new test) — parses `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt`, partitions rsIDs into non-`kgp*` and `kgp*` sets, regenerates the mini bundle into `tmp_path`, and asserts (i) every non-`kgp*` rsID is present in `vep_annotations`, and (ii) no `kgp*` rsID is present (so step 40's coordinate-fallback regression assertion has a deterministic miss to exercise). Tightens the existing module so a future fixture or seed-CSV edit that drops AncestryDNA coverage trips at test time. The pre-existing `test_mini_vep_bundle_has_data` (≥50 rows) and `test_mini_vep_bundle_carries_v2_0_0_metadata` (Phase 0 schema/version alignment) continue to pass — the new test layers rsID-coverage on top of the row-count + metadata invariants without changing them.

##### Notes

- Scope discipline (per the per-step PR convention): only `tests/fixtures/seed_csvs/vep_seed.csv`, `tests/fixtures/mini_vep_bundle.db`, `tests/backend/test_regenerate_fixtures.py`, and `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry) are touched. No production source files, no Alembic migrations, no schema declarations, no scripts. The 2 `kgp*` rows in `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` (`kgp12345678 1 2000000 A G`, `kgp98765432 2 3000000 C T`) are deliberately *not* added to the seed — they exercise the coordinate-fallback path that step 40 (ADNA-09) asserts via `coverage_stats["vep_bundle_coord_fallback_hits"] >= kgp_count`. Any future seed edit that accidentally pulls them in trips the new test's negative assertion.
- Step 39 is not on the canonical full-sweep list (CLAUDE.md SOP #8 — full-sweep set: 8, 13, 17, 29, 46, 54, 61, 62, 63, 64, 65, 66; phase boundaries: 18, 19, 45, 59, 87). It touches no Python source files, no migrations, no per-sample schema declarations — only the fixture-DB regeneration surface. Targeted local sweep: `pytest tests/backend/test_regenerate_fixtures.py` — 34 cases green (33 pre-step-39 + 1 new). Companion sweep of every importer of `mini_vep_bundle.db` / `vep_annotations` — `pytest tests/backend/test_vep_bundle_lookup.py tests/backend/test_annotation_engine.py tests/backend/test_e2e_pipeline.py tests/backend/test_cross_module_integration.py tests/backend/test_variant_detail_api.py tests/backend/test_build_vep_bundle.py` — all 240 cases still green; nothing downstream depended on the prior ~100-row mini-bundle size. Ruff clean on the touched test file.
- Risk-register touch points (Plan §1.3): **R-04** (annotation pipeline correctness) — the mini bundle now deterministically covers every non-`kgp*` rsID in the canonical AncestryDNA fixture, which is the prerequisite for step 40's PR-blocking annotation regression test (`hit_rate == 1 - kgp_count / total_variants` for rsID matches, plus the `kgp*` coord-fallback assertion). **R-19** (test-fixture provenance) — every new seed row is derived deterministically from the committed `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` rsID + coordinate space; no consultation of the local-only real export. The placeholder synthetic ref/alt/consequence values are not user-facing data, and the existing rsIDs with real annotations are not overwritten.

#### Step 38 — 23andMe dispatcher regression

##### Added

- `tests/backend/test_parser_23andme.py::TestDispatcherRegressionFor23andMe` (new class, 10 cases; ADNA-08d; Plan §13.1, §8.7) — locks the post-step-29 invariant that routing a 23andMe input through `backend.ingestion.dispatcher.parse` returns the same `base.ParseResult` as calling `parse_23andme` directly, with no dispatcher-side transformation in between:
  - `test_dispatcher_parse_matches_direct_call` — 3-case `pytest.parametrize` block over the canonical v3/v4/v5 fixtures (`sample_23andme_v3.txt` → version `"v3"` / build `GRCh36` / 100 variants; `sample_23andme_v4.txt` → `"v4"` / `GRCh37` / 100; `sample_23andme_v5.txt` → `"v5"` / `GRCh37` / 1000). For each fixture asserts `dispatcher.parse(fixture) == parse_23andme(fixture)` along every dimension Plan §13.1 ADNA-08d names — vendor identity (`SourceVendor.TWENTYTHREEANDME`), string version, build, total variant count — plus byte-identical `variants` list parity (locks against any future re-order / transform on the dispatcher hop) and matching `nocall_count` / `total_lines` / `skipped_lines` (guards against the dispatcher's head-line read double-counting header or no-call rows downstream of itself).
  - `test_v5_file_format_composition_matches_plan_8_7` — locks the Plan §8.7 `samples.file_format = f"{vendor.value}_{version}"` composition through the dispatcher: `dispatcher.parse(V5_FILE)` composes to `"23andme_v5"`. A change to either the `SourceVendor` enum value or the parser version string trips here at the caller-visible surface, not just inside the parser.
  - `test_dispatcher_side_helpers_absent_from_parser_23andme` — 3-case `pytest.parametrize` block locking ADNA-08d's second clause: `parser_23andme._looks_like_23andme`, `parser_23andme._looks_like_ancestrydna`, and `parser_23andme._reject_with_guidance` all `hasattr` → False. Vendor-routing predicates and the format-guidance fallback live in `dispatcher`; this asserts they have not drifted back into the bare 23andMe parser. `_detect_format` is deliberately *not* in the parametrize list because it is a vendor-internal *version* detector (v3/v4/v5), not a vendor-dispatch helper — Plan ADNA-08d permits it on the parser module.
  - `test_dispatcher_side_helpers_present_on_dispatcher` — negative-sibling 3-case `pytest.parametrize` block asserting `dispatcher._looks_like_23andme`, `dispatcher._looks_like_ancestrydna`, and the public `dispatcher.detect_vendor` all `hasattr` → True. Without this, the absence-on-parser assertion above could trivially pass by way of the helpers having simply vanished from the codebase; pairing both sides locks the helpers' *location*, not just their non-presence.

##### Notes

- Scope discipline (per the per-step PR convention): only `tests/backend/test_parser_23andme.py` (extended) and `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry) are touched. Production parser / dispatcher code is unchanged — every new assertion passes against the existing `parse_23andme` + `dispatcher.parse` implementations as they landed in steps 27–29, which proves the dispatcher hop is already transparent for 23andMe inputs and the helper boundary between `parser_23andme` and `dispatcher` is correctly drawn. The companion AncestryDNA-side dispatcher regression (`TestDispatcherFlipForAncestryDNA`, step 33) remains in place; together the two classes pin both vendors of the dispatcher's routing matrix on the same module.
- Step 38 is not on the canonical full-sweep list (CLAUDE.md SOP #8 — full-sweep set: 8, 13, 17, 29, 46, 54, 61, 62, 63, 64, 65, 66; phase boundaries: 18, 19, 45, 59, 87). It touches one existing test file and no production / schema / migration surface. Targeted local sweep: `pytest tests/backend/test_parser_23andme.py` — 53 cases green (43 pre-step-38 + 10 new); companion `pytest tests/backend/test_dispatcher.py` re-run — all 15 pre-existing cases still green. Ruff clean (`ruff check tests/backend/test_parser_23andme.py` + `ruff format --check`).
- Relation to companion classes: `TestNoDispatchHelpers` (landed in step 29) locks that `_reject_non_23andme` / `_check_binary` / `detect_format` were retired from `parser_23andme` and that `parse_23andme` + `normalize_chromosome` are the only `__all__`-exposed names. `TestDispatcherRegressionFor23andMe` (this step) layers (i) the dispatcher-hop equivalence assertion on top of that surface, and (ii) extends the surface audit to the dispatcher-side `_looks_like_*` predicates with a both-sides location lock that step 29's class did not need.
- Risk-register touch points (Plan §1.3): **R-04** (parser correctness) — every assertion lands on existing parser + dispatcher code paths, so this step is purely additive surface that hardens the post-step-29 contract; no parser, dispatcher, annotation engine, ingest-route, or schema surface changes. **R-19** (test-fixture provenance) is not engaged — every input is one of the committed `sample_23andme_v{3,4,5}.txt` fixtures already on `main`, with no consultation of the local-only real export.

#### Step 37 — Parser raise-path tests

##### Added

- `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna_raise_paths.py` (new file; ADNA-08e; Plan §13.1, §8.6) — table-driven coverage for every `MalformedDataError` cause the AncestryDNA parser promises to catch plus the two parse-time canonicalization rules from Plan §8.6:
  - `test_raises_malformed_data_error` — 7-case `pytest.parametrize` block, one entry per Plan §13.1 ADNA-08e raise path: (a) empty rsid → `match="empty rsid"`; (b) non-numeric position (`"notanumber"`) → `match="non-numeric position"`; (c) negative position (`-100`) → `match="negative position"`; (d) invalid chromosome `27` (outside the AncestryDNA 1–26 range) → `match="Invalid chromosome value"`; (e) wrong column count, 4 columns → `match="expected 5 columns"`; (f) wrong column count, 6 columns → `match="expected 5 columns"`; (g) whitespace-only rsid (`"   "`) → also `match="empty rsid"` (locked separately so a future parser that skipped the per-field strip would still trip). Each input is fed through a minimal in-memory `_stream()` helper that prepends the `#AncestryDNA` signature + 5-column header, so the assertion lands on `_validate_line` / `normalize_for`, not the dispatcher.
  - `test_element_wise_no_call_rule` — 7-case `pytest.parametrize` block locking Plan §8.6 #2's per-allele no-call rule through the public `parse_ancestrydna` entry point: `I/0`, `0/I`, `D/0`, `0/D`, `A/0`, `0/G`, and whitespace-then-SNV (` /T`) all canonicalize to `"--"` and bump `nocall_count` to 1. Parallels `_canonical_genotype`'s helper-level coverage in `test_parser_ancestrydna.py`; this test asserts the end-to-end parse path so a regression that bypasses the helper inside `_validate_line` still trips.
  - `test_sorted_pair_canonicalization` — 6-case `pytest.parametrize` block locking Plan §8.6 #6 + #7 storage normalization at the parse-result level: `G/A` and `A/G` both store as `"AG"`; `I/D` and `D/I` both store as `"DI"`; lowercase `g/A` and `A/g` both uppercase-then-sort to `"AG"`. Each row also asserts `nocall_count == 0` so a regression that misroutes a canonical-form input through the no-call path still trips.

##### Notes

- Scope discipline (per the per-step PR convention): only `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna_raise_paths.py` (new test file) and `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry) are touched. Production parser code is unchanged — every new test passes against the existing `parse_ancestrydna` implementation, which proves the parser already honors Plan §8.6 #2 / #6 / #7 raise paths and canonicalization rules. The dispatcher unit tests called for under Plan §13.1 ADNA-08b ship separately in their own file; this step's scope is the AncestryDNA parser's raise-path + canonicalization contract through the public entry point.
- Relation to companion file: `test_parser_ancestrydna.py` already carries inline raise-path smoke tests (`test_wrong_column_count_raises`, `test_empty_rsid_raises`, `test_invalid_chromosome_raises`, `test_non_numeric_position_raises`) plus the helper-level `_canonical_genotype` parametrize block. The new `test_parser_ancestrydna_raise_paths.py` is the table-driven, ADNA-08e-checklist-exhaustive sibling: it extends the raise-path coverage to cases the smoke tests omit (negative position, whitespace-only rsid, wrong-column-count-of-6), and it pins the canonicalization contract through the public `parse_ancestrydna` entry rather than the `_canonical_genotype` helper, so a regression that bypasses the helper inside the parse body still trips.
- Step 37 is not on the canonical full-sweep list (CLAUDE.md SOP #8 — full-sweep set: 8, 13, 17, 29, 46, 54, 61, 62, 63, 64, 65, 66; phase boundaries: 18, 19, 45, 59, 87). It touches a single new test file and no production / schema / migration surface. Targeted local sweep: `pytest tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna_raise_paths.py` — all 20 cases green; companion `pytest tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py` re-run — all 43 cases still green. Ruff clean on the new file.
- Risk-register touch points (Plan §1.3): **R-04** (parser correctness) — every assertion lands on the existing parser code path, so this step is purely additive surface that hardens the contract; no parser, dispatcher, annotation engine, or schema surface changes. **R-19** (test-fixture provenance) is not engaged — every input is synthesized inline as an `io.StringIO`, with no fixture-file dependency and no consultation of the local-only real export.

#### Step 36 — Positive parser tests + CRLF + non-UTF-8 byte assertions

##### Added

- `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py::TestParseV2Fixture::test_chr25_par_rows_collapse_to_x` — locks Plan §8.6 #4 against every chr25 PAR row in `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` (rs5778923 + the four step-34 stride samples rs28736870 / rs397514462 / rs7205 / rs17842875). Asserts each lands on chromosome `"X"` after parsing, and that no `ParsedVariant.chrom == "25"` row survives — protects against a regression that silently leaves a subset of PAR rows unmapped.
- `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py::TestParseV2Fixture::test_chr26_rows_normalize_to_mt` — parallel coverage for the chr26 → `"MT"` normalization across all 11 chr26 fixture rows (the locked rs9999003 plus the ten step-34 sampled MT rsIDs). Asserts no `ParsedVariant.chrom == "26"` row survives.
- `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py::TestParseV2Fixture::test_full_00_no_call_increments_nocall_count` — explicit single-row assertion that the full `0`/`0` row (rs9999001 on chr1) canonicalizes to `"--"` and contributes to `nocall_count`. Sibling of the existing `test_no_calls_canonicalized` set-shape assertion; locks the per-row contract so a regression that flips the count without changing the canonical sentinel still trips.
- `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py::TestParseV2Fixture::test_kgp_rsids_in_fixture_pass_through_verbatim` — fixture-row assertion that both `kgp12345678` (chr1 pos 2000000 → `"AG"`) and `kgp98765432` (chr2 pos 3000000 → `"CT"`) survive the parse byte-identical to the raw export. Complements the inline `test_kgp_rsids_pass_through_verbatim` smoke test by anchoring to the fixture rows used in step 40's annotation-engine coverage regression.
- `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py::TestCommittedFixtureParity::test_crlf_fixture_parses_identically_to_lf` — parses the committed `sample_ancestrydna_crlf.txt` (the bit-for-bit `\r\n` rewrite landed in step 35) and asserts every `ParseResult` field matches `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt`: `vendor`, `version`, `build`, the full `variants` list (order + values), `nocall_count`, `total_lines`, `skipped_lines`. Replaces the inline `test_crlf_line_endings` tmp_path synthetic-CRLF case as the load-bearing assertion for Plan §8.6 #8 — the inline smoke test stays as a defense against breakages in the round-trip rewrite path, but the fixture-file test is the regression-blocker if someone re-saves the committed fixture without CRLF.
- `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py::TestCommittedFixtureParity::test_non_utf8_byte_fixture_variants_byte_identical_to_lf` — parses the committed `sample_ancestrydna_non_utf8_byte.txt` (the stray-`\xff`-in-comment-line-1 copy landed in step 35) and asserts `vendor == ANCESTRYDNA`, `version == "v2.0"`, `build == "GRCh37"`, plus byte-identical `variants` / `nocall_count` / `total_lines` / `skipped_lines` against the LF fixture. Locks the `open(..., encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")` contract from Plan §8.6 #9 against the committed fixture rather than against an inline-injected stray byte.
- `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py::test_truncated_fixture_parses_to_expected_counts` — writes the head-50 lines of `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` (8 comment + 1 header + 41 data rows) into a tmp file, parses it, and asserts `total_lines == 50`, `skipped_lines == 9`, `len(variants) == 41`, `total_lines == skipped_lines + len(variants)`, first row is `rs4477212` on chr1, and both `kgp*` IDs (lines 37 + 38) are present in the parsed list. Covers ADNA-08's "truncated fixture parses to expected counts" requirement — locks the parser against a regression that would emit a misleading total/variant-count mismatch on a partial download.

##### Notes

- Scope discipline (per the per-step PR convention): only `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py` (test extension) and `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry) are touched. The committed CRLF + non-UTF-8 fixtures were already landed in step 35 — no fixture-file changes here. Production parser code is unchanged: every new test passes against the existing `parse_ancestrydna` implementation, which proves the parser already honors Plan §8.6 #8–9 against the committed fixtures (the new tests are the missing assertion surface, not driving new behavior).
- The two pre-existing inline tests (`test_crlf_line_endings`, `test_non_utf8_byte_in_comment_replaced`) are kept alongside the new fixture-file `TestCommittedFixtureParity` class. They cover complementary surfaces — the inline tests assert the parser handles *synthetic* CRLF / stray-byte payloads regardless of the committed fixtures; the fixture-file tests assert the parser handles the *committed* fixtures regardless of any synthetic generator. Together they catch both implementation regressions and fixture-curation regressions.

#### Step 35 — Auxiliary AncestryDNA fixtures

##### Added

- `tests/fixtures/sample_ancestrydna_malformed.txt` (Plan §16.1) — 5-row corruption fixture for the step-37 raise-path tests. Carries the four corruption variants step 35 declares: a valid baseline row (`rs1000001 1 100000 A G`) followed by the four malformed cases — **missing column** (`rs1000002 1 200000 C`, 4 fields not 5), **non-numeric position** (`rs1000003 1 notanumber G G`), **invalid chromosome `27`** (`rs1000004 27 300000 T T` — outside the 1–26 AncestryDNA range), and **empty rsid** (leading `\t1\t400000\tA\tA` — first field is the empty string). Header banner is the canonical 8-comment + 5-column header block; comment text is byte-identical to `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` lines 1–8. The fixture intentionally omits negative-position / wrong-column-count-6 / whitespace-only-rsid / element-wise-no-call / sorted-pair-canonicalization / mixed-case cases — step 37's table-driven raise-path tests will drive those inline via `io.StringIO`, not from this file.
- `tests/fixtures/sample_ancestrydna_crlf.txt` (Plan §16.1, §8.6 #8) — bit-for-bit copy of `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` with every `\n` rewritten to `\r\n` (598 CR + 598 LF, total 16,340 bytes vs. v2's 15,742). Locks the Plan §8.6 #8 CRLF-tolerance contract: step 36's positive-parser tests assert the resulting `ParseResult` (vendor, version, build, variants list, counts) is byte-identical to the LF fixture's. Generated via a one-shot `src.replace(b"\n", b"\r\n")`; the v2 fixture was first asserted CR-free (`src.count(b"\r") == 0`) so the rewrite is clean and not a re-conversion of already-mixed line endings.
- `tests/fixtures/sample_ancestrydna_non_utf8_byte.txt` (Plan §16.1, §8.6 #9) — bit-for-bit copy of `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` with a single stray `\xff` byte injected mid-comment on line 1 (between `#AncestryDNA` and ` raw data download\n`). 15,743 bytes (v2 + 1). Locks the `open(..., encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")` contract from Plan §8.6 #9: step 36's positive-parser tests assert the parse completes without raising and the variant list is byte-identical to the clean LF fixture. The 0xff sits inside the comment header that the parser skips, so the stray byte never reaches a data row; verified at fixture-write time via `read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace").replace("�", "") == v2_text`.

##### Notes

- Scope discipline (per the per-step PR convention): only the three fixture files are added. No production sources, no test files, no documentation outside this CHANGELOG entry are touched. The positive-parser CRLF + non-UTF-8-byte assertions (Plan §8.6 #8–9) land in step 36 (`tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py` extension); the table-driven raise-path tests (empty rsid, non-numeric position, invalid chromosome `27`, etc.) land in step 37 (`tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna_raise_paths.py`). Neither is in scope here.
- Step 35 is not on the canonical full-sweep list (CLAUDE.md SOP #8 — full-sweep set: 8, 13, 17, 29, 46, 54, 61, 62, 63, 64, 65, 66; phase boundaries: 18, 19, 45, 59, 87). It touches no Python / TypeScript code, no migrations, no schema declarations — only three new static fixture files in `tests/fixtures/`. A `grep -rn "sample_ancestrydna_malformed\|sample_ancestrydna_crlf\|sample_ancestrydna_non_utf8" --include='*.py' --include='*.ts' --include='*.tsx'` of the source tree returns zero hits, confirming nothing currently loads these fixtures; the targeted-test surface is empty. Verification was fixture-write-time round-trip checks (CRLF-rewrite identity, `errors="replace"` equivalence, 5-row corruption parse).
- Risk-register touch points (Plan §1.3): **R-19** (test-fixture provenance) — every byte of every fixture is either synthesized inline (the malformed file's 5 hand-written rows) or a deterministic transform of the already-synthesized `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` (CRLF byte-rewrite, single-byte `\xff` injection in a comment line). The real `AncestryDNA.txt` export is not consulted by this step; no genotype field is copied from it. **R-04** is not engaged — no parser, dispatcher, annotation engine, or schema surface changes; existing test assertions are unaffected because nothing references the new files yet.
- Ordering: the three fixtures are prerequisites for steps 36 (`test_parser_ancestrydna.py` positive CRLF + non-UTF-8-byte assertions) and 37 (`test_parser_ancestrydna_raise_paths.py` table-driven `MalformedDataError` cases). Landing step 35 ahead of those steps keeps each subsequent PR's diff scoped to test code only.

#### Step 34 — Curate `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` fixture

##### Changed

- `tests/fixtures/sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` (Plan §16.1) — expanded from the 35-row minimum that step 33 shipped to **589 data rows** (8 comment lines + 1 header + 589 data = 598 total lines), hitting the Plan §16.1 "500–1000 rsIDs" target. The 35-row locked block (APOE `rs429358`/`rs7412`, MTHFR `rs1801131`/`rs1801133`, no-call set `{rs2032597, rs9999001}`, chrX `rs6655587`, sorted-pair locus `rs3892097`, chrY hemizygous `rs9999050`, PAR `rs5778923`, MT `rs9999003`, indels `rs9999004`–`rs9999007` in both `I/D` and `D/I` orderings, legacy `kgp12345678`/`kgp98765432`) sits unchanged at the top of the file so every step-33 test assertion stays byte-identical green. 554 new rows are stride-sampled across the 26 raw AncestryDNA chromosomes (1–22 / 23-X / 24-Y / 25-PAR / 26-MT) directly from the local-only real V2.0 export's coordinate space — **coordinates only**; every genotype field is deterministically re-synthesized via `md5("{rsid}|{chrom}|{pos}") → {A,C,G,T}²` per Plan §16.2's "bio-validator hand-picks coordinates from the export but regenerates every genotype field synthetically" guard-rail. chrY (raw `24`) and MT (raw `26`) rows are forced homozygous to match the §8.6 #3 hemizygous-on-haploid contract. Sampled rows never introduce additional no-calls or indels, so `nocall_count == 2` and the indel-coverage edge-case rows stay the canonical four. Chromosome budget (sampled, before chr-25→X / chr-26→MT collapse): chr1=35, chr2=35, chr3=30, chr4=28, chr5=28, chr6=30, chr7=25, chr8=25, chr9=22, chr10=25, chr11=25, chr12=25, chr13=20, chr14=18, chr15=18, chr16=20, chr17=20, chr18=16, chr19=14, chr20=16, chr21=10, chr22=12, X=25, Y=18, PAR=4, MT=10.
- `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py::TestParseV2Fixture::test_variant_count_matches_data_rows` — updated row-count assertions from `len(result.variants) == 35` / `total_lines == 44` to `== 589` / `== 598`; `skipped_lines == 9` is unchanged (header/comment block is byte-identical). Docstring rewritten to name the 35-row locked block + 554-row hand-curated sample, and to re-cite the Plan §16.2 synthesized-genotype guard-rail. Every other case (`test_no_calls_canonicalized`, `test_apoe_rsids_present`, `test_chr_x_call_preserved`, `test_sorted_pair_canonicalization_on_data`, `test_result_shape`) stays byte-identical green — the locked block preserves their reference rsIDs, genotypes, and nocall_count.

##### Notes

- Curation: a one-off, **not-committed** Python helper read the local-only `AncestryDNA.txt` (excluded by `.gitignore` per Plan §16.2's "Never committed" guard-rail), bucketed real rows by chromosome, applied an even-stride sampler within each bucket, and synthesized every emitted genotype from the (rsid, chrom, pos) hash. The script's only inputs are positional metadata; it does not read column 4 or 5 of the real export. Discarded after the fixture landed — future re-curations recompute deterministically from the same coordinate set.
- Locked-row preservation: the four named test assertions in `TestParseV2Fixture` (APOE `TT`/`CC`, chrX `rs6655587 AG`, sorted-pair `rs3892097 AG`, no-call set `{rs2032597, rs9999001}` with `nocall_count == 2`) are anchor points — every one survives because the 35-row block is reproduced verbatim and the 554 new rows neither shadow nor pollute it. Synthesizer collision-checked against `LOCKED_RSIDS` and `LOCKED_COORDS` before emission.
- Scope discipline (per the per-step PR convention): only the fixture + the one parser test that locks its row count are touched. No production source files change. The mini VEP bundle is regenerated to cover this fixture's rsIDs in step 39 (ADNA-09 prerequisite); the PR-blocking annotation regression is step 40; the synthetic EUR full fixture (`synthetic_eur_ancestrydna.txt`) lands in step 41 via `scripts/regenerate_fixtures.py --vendor=ancestrydna`; auxiliary fixtures (`sample_ancestrydna_malformed.txt`, `sample_ancestrydna_crlf.txt`, `sample_ancestrydna_non_utf8_byte.txt`) land in step 35.
- Risk-register touch points (Plan §1.3): **R-19** (test-fixture provenance) — every genotype is synthesized from a deterministic hash of positional metadata; the real export is consulted for `(rsid, chrom, pos)` triples only and is never copied byte-for-byte into a fixture file. **R-04** (annotation pipeline regression — fixture-shape stability) — the locked 35-row block guarantees every step-33 assertion stays byte-identical green; the new sampled rows have all-standard SNV genotypes on autosomes / X / Y / PAR / MT so downstream consumers (`test_bundle_gating.py`, `test_dispatcher.py`, `test_generate_vep_input.py`, `test_lai_runner_ancestrydna.py`) keep their bounded `variant_count > 0` contracts.
- Targeted local sweep (per CLAUDE.md SOP #8): step 34 is not on the canonical full-sweep list. Ran `pytest tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py tests/backend/test_parser_23andme.py tests/backend/test_dispatcher.py tests/backend/test_generate_vep_input.py tests/backend/test_lai_runner_ancestrydna.py tests/backend/test_bundle_gating.py tests/backend/test_lai.py` — all green except the pre-existing `TestRealBundleLAIAccuracy::test_global_ancestry_within_one_percent_of_reference` failure, which is a slow-tier nightly-only marker (`@pytest.mark.slow @pytest.mark.requires_real_bundle @pytest.mark.requires_java`) that auto-skips on CI and stock dev machines but locally surfaces here because Java is on PATH and a real LAI bundle is extracted under `data_dir`. The failure pre-dates step 34 (confirmed by `git stash` revert + re-run) and remains dormant until step 41 lands `synthetic_eur_ancestrydna.txt` per the test's fixture-candidate list. Ruff clean on `test_parser_ancestrydna.py`.

#### Step 33 — Migrate legacy fixture + flip rejection test

##### Changed

- `tests/fixtures/sample_ancestrydna.txt` (ADNA-08a; Plan §13.1) — **deleted.** Superseded by `tests/fixtures/sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt` (35 data rows, 8 comment lines + 1 header, 44 total lines; 2 no-calls: `rs2032597` chrY `C/0` partial + `rs9999001` chr1 `0/0` full). The new fixture keeps the legacy row contract (APOE `rs429358`/`rs7412` on chr19; MTHFR `rs1801131`/`rs1801133` on chr1; sorted-pair locus `rs3892097 G/A → "AG"`; chrX `rs6655587`) and layers in the Plan §8.6 edge-case checklist: `00` full no-call (#1), partial `C/0` no-call (#2), hemizygous chrY `A/A` (#3 — new row `rs9999050`), PAR `chr25 → X` collapse at PAR1 position 60123 (#4 — new row `rs5778923`, well separated from the chrX `rs6655587` PAR boundary at 2699555), chr26 → MT homozygous-on-haploid (`rs9999003`), indels in both `I/D` and `D/I` orderings plus homozygous `II`/`DD` (#6 — new rows `rs9999004`–`rs9999007`), and legacy `kgp*` passthrough (#7 — new rows `kgp12345678` / `kgp98765432` on chr1/chr2). The fixture is the minimum sufficient to make every step-33 test green; step 34 will expand it to bio-validator's 500–1000 rsID curation from the real V2.0 export (Plan §16.1).
- `tests/backend/test_parser_ancestrydna.py` — `LEGACY_FIXTURE` → `FIXTURE_V2`; `TestParseLegacyFixture` → `TestParseV2Fixture`. Updated row-count assertions (`len(result.variants) == 35`, `total_lines == 44`, `skipped_lines == 9`) and renamed `test_partial_no_call_canonicalized` → `test_no_calls_canonicalized` (now asserts the no-call set is exactly `{"rs2032597", "rs9999001"}` and `nocall_count == 2`, covering Plan §8.6 #1 + #2 in one case). The APOE / chrX / sorted-pair assertions stay byte-identical green. The in-memory edge-case + raise-path test surfaces are unchanged (still drive `io.StringIO` payloads).
- `tests/backend/test_bundle_gating.py` — `ANCESTRY_FILE` rebound to `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt`. The three §5.4 bundle-gate cases (`test_ancestrydna_with_v1_bundle_returns_409`, `test_ancestrydna_with_v2_bundle_returns_202`, `test_23andme_with_v1_bundle_returns_202`) now exercise the dispatcher → `parser_ancestrydna` end-to-end against the v2 fixture; the variant-count assertion is the existing `body["variant_count"] > 0` so the contract holds with 35 rows just as it did with 20.
- `tests/backend/test_dispatcher.py::test_detect_vendor_ancestrydna_fixture` — fixture path rebound to `sample_ancestrydna_v2.txt`. The other 14 dispatcher cases (header-only detection, precedence, rejection-with-guidance, stream contract, unified `parse()` shape) stay byte-identical green.

The `vendor-ancestrydna` parametrize case's `skipif` reason was updated to name step 33 as the v2 fixture's landing step. The other test surfaces (`--rsid-catalog` mode, 23andMe parse path, CLI round-trip) stay byte-identical green.

##### Tests

#### Step 31 — Ingest route → dispatcher

##### Changed

- `backend/api/routes/ingest.py` (ADNA-05; Plan §8.7) — switched the route's parser entry point from `parser_23andme.parse_23andme` to `backend.ingestion.dispatcher.parse`. The import becomes `from backend.ingestion.dispatcher import ParserError, parse`; `_ingest_file` calls `parse(io.StringIO(text))` and composes the persisted `samples.file_format` (and `sample_metadata.file_format`) value as `f"{result.vendor.value}_{result.version}"` — yields the existing `"23andme_v5"` for 23andMe uploads and `"ancestrydna_v2.0"` for AncestryDNA uploads. The composed value is computed once and reused for the `samples` insert, the `sample_metadata_table` insert, and the response payload so a future vendor addition only changes one site. The bundle-version §5.4 gate (step 7 `_sniff_is_ancestrydna` + `_vep_bundle_blocks_ancestrydna`) is intentionally untouched — it remains the pre-parse 409 surface on AncestryDNA uploads against pre-`v2.0.0` bundles, ahead of the dispatcher running.
- `backend/ingestion/dispatcher.py` — re-exported `ParserError` (imported from `backend.ingestion.base`) so the ingest route's single-symbol import line from Plan §8.7 (`from backend.ingestion.dispatcher import parse, ParserError`) resolves without dipping into `base`. `__all__` updated to `["ParserError", "detect_vendor", "parse"]`.
- Public route docstring updated to read "Upload and parse a 23andMe or AncestryDNA raw data file" and to name `dispatcher.parse` as the routing surface; the §5.4 gate behavior description is unchanged.

##### Tests

- `tests/backend/test_bundle_gating.py::test_ancestrydna_with_v2_bundle_returns_202` — removed the `patch("backend.api.routes.ingest.parse_23andme", return_value=fake_result)` stub introduced in step 7. With step 30's `parser_ancestrydna` landed and step 31 wiring the dispatcher into the route, the real AncestryDNA parser now runs end-to-end on the legacy `tests/fixtures/sample_ancestrydna.txt`. Test now asserts `response.status_code == 202`, `body["variant_count"] > 0` (real parser output rather than the synthetic single-variant fake), and `body["file_format"] == "ancestrydna_v2.0"` — the load-bearing new assertion that locks the `f"{vendor.value}_{version}"` composition this step ships. The obsolete `ParsedVariant` / `ParseResult` / `SourceVendor` imports were removed alongside the stub. The other two §5.4 cases (`test_ancestrydna_with_v1_bundle_returns_409`, `test_23andme_with_v1_bundle_returns_202`) stay byte-identical green.

##### Notes
